1.1 Overview {#Overview .indexable data-level="2"}					1.1 Overview {#Overview .indexable data-level="2"}
------------										------------

The scope of this Protection Profile ([PP](#abbr_PP)) is to describe the		The scope of this Protection Profile ([PP](#abbr_PP)) is to describe the
security functionality of application software in terms of				security functionality of application software in terms of
[\[CC\]](#bibCC) and to define functional and assurance requirements for		[\[CC\]](#bibCC) and to define functional and assurance requirements for
such software. In recent years, software attacks have shifted from			such software. In recent years, software attacks have shifted from
targeting operating systems to targeting applications. This has been the		targeting operating systems to targeting applications. This has been the
natural response to improvements in operating system security and			natural response to improvements in operating system security and
development processes. As a result, it is paramount that the security of		development processes. As a result, it is paramount that the security of
applications be improved to reduce the risk of compromise.				applications be improved to reduce the risk of compromise.

3.1 Threats {#Threats .indexable data-level="2"}					3.1 Threats {#Threats .indexable data-level="2"}
-----------										-----------

T.NETWORK\_ATTACK									T.NETWORK\_ATTACK
:   An attacker is positioned on a communications channel or elsewhere			:   An attacker is positioned on a communications channel or elsewhere
    on the network infrastructure. Attackers may engage in				    on the network infrastructure. Attackers may engage in
    communications with the application software or alter communications		    communications with the application software or alter communications
    between the application software and other endpoints in order to			    between the application software and other endpoints in order to
    compromise it.									    compromise it.

T.NETWORK\_EAVESDROP									T.NETWORK\_EAVESDROP
:   An attacker is positioned on a communications channel or elsewhere			:   An attacker is positioned on a communications channel or elsewhere
    on the network infrastructure. Attackers may monitor and gain access		    on the network infrastructure. Attackers may monitor and gain access
    to data exchanged between the application and other endpoints.			    to data exchanged between the application and other endpoints.

T.LOCAL\_ATTACK										T.LOCAL\_ATTACK
:   An attacker can act through unprivileged software on the same			:   An attacker can act through unprivileged software on the same
    computing platform on which the application executes. Attackers may			    computing platform on which the application executes. Attackers may
    provide maliciously formatted input to the application in the form			    provide maliciously formatted input to the application in the form
    of files or other local communications.						    of files or other local communications.

T.PHYSICAL\_ACCESS									T.PHYSICAL\_ACCESS
:   An attacker may try to access sensitive data at rest.				:   An attacker may try to access sensitive data at rest.

---------------										---------------

:   The [TOE](#abbr_TOE) relies upon a trustworthy computing platform			:   The [TOE](#abbr_TOE) relies upon a trustworthy computing platform
    with a reliable time clock for its execution. This includes the			    with a reliable time clock for its execution. This includes the
    underlying platform and whatever runtime environment it provides to			    underlying platform and whatever runtime environment it provides to
    the [TOE](#abbr_TOE).								    the [TOE](#abbr_TOE).

    hostile, and uses the software in compliance with the applied			    hostile, and uses the software in compliance with the applied
    enterprise security policy.								    enterprise security policy.

4 Security Objectives {#Security_Objectives .indexable data-level="1"}			4 Security Objectives {#Security_Objectives .indexable data-level="1"}
=====================									=====================

4.1 Security Objectives for the TOE {#Security_Objectives_for_the_TOE .indexable data	4.1 Security Objectives for the TOE {#Security_Objectives_for_the_TOE .indexable data
-----------------------------------							-----------------------------------

O.INTEGRITY										O.INTEGRITY
:   Conformant TOEs ensure the integrity of their installation and			:   Conformant TOEs ensure the integrity of their installation and
    update packages, and also leverage execution environment-based			    update packages, and also leverage execution environment-based
    mitigations. Software is seldom, if ever, shipped without errors.			    mitigations. Software is seldom, if ever, shipped without errors.
    The ability to deploy patches and updates to fielded software with			    The ability to deploy patches and updates to fielded software with
    integrity is critical to enterprise network security. Processor			    integrity is critical to enterprise network security. Processor
    manufacturers, compiler developers, execution environment vendors,			    manufacturers, compiler developers, execution environment vendors,
    and operating system vendors have developed execution				    and operating system vendors have developed execution
    environment-based mitigations that increase the cost to attackers by		    environment-based mitigations that increase the cost to attackers by
    adding complexity to the task of compromising systems. Application			    adding complexity to the task of compromising systems. Application
    software can often take advantage of these mechanisms by using APIs			    software can often take advantage of these mechanisms by using APIs
    provided by the runtime environment or by enabling the mechanism			    provided by the runtime environment or by enabling the mechanism
    through compiler or linker options.							    through compiler or linker options.

O.QUALITY										O.QUALITY
:   To ensure quality of implementation, conformant TOEs leverage			:   To ensure quality of implementation, conformant TOEs leverage
    services and APIs provided by the runtime environment rather than			    services and APIs provided by the runtime environment rather than
    implementing their own versions of these services and APIs. This is			    implementing their own versions of these services and APIs. This is
    especially important for cryptographic services and other complex			    especially important for cryptographic services and other complex
    operations such as file and media parsing. Leveraging this platform			    operations such as file and media parsing. Leveraging this platform
    behavior relies upon using only documented and supported APIs.			    behavior relies upon using only documented and supported APIs.

O.MANAGEMENT										O.MANAGEMENT
:   To facilitate management by users and the enterprise, conformant			:   To facilitate management by users and the enterprise, conformant
    TOEs provide consistent and supported interfaces for their				    TOEs provide consistent and supported interfaces for their
    security-relevant configuration and maintenance. This includes the			    security-relevant configuration and maintenance. This includes the
    deployment of applications and application updates through the use			    deployment of applications and application updates through the use
    of platform-supported deployment mechanisms and formats, as well as			    of platform-supported deployment mechanisms and formats, as well as
    providing mechanisms for configuration. This also includes providing		    providing mechanisms for configuration. This also includes providing
    control to the user regarding disclosure of any [PII](#abbr_PII).			    control to the user regarding disclosure of any [PII](#abbr_PII).

O.PROTECTED\_STORAGE									O.PROTECTED\_STORAGE
:   To address the issue of loss of confidentiality of user data in the			:   To address the issue of loss of confidentiality of user data in the
    event of loss of physical control of the storage medium, conformant			    event of loss of physical control of the storage medium, conformant

D.3 Specific Guidance for Determining Product Model Equivalence {#modelequiv .indexab	D.3 Specific Guidance for Determining Product Model Equivalence {#modelequiv .indexab
---------------------------------------------------------------				---------------------------------------------------------------

Product Model equivalence attempts to determine whether different			Product Model equivalence attempts to determine whether different
feature levels of the same product across a product line are equivalent			feature levels of the same product across a product line are equivalent
for purposes of [PP](#abbr_PP) testing. For example, if a product has a			for purposes of [PP](#abbr_PP) testing. For example, if a product has a
"basic" edition and an "enterprise" edition, is it necessary to test			"basic" edition and an "enterprise" edition, is it necessary to test
both models? Or does testing one model provide sufficient assurance that		both models? Or does testing one model provide sufficient assurance that
